[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as an AddressSanitizer SEGV error with a scariness score of [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mwild-addr-read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating a severe memory safety violation. The crash occurs [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring the processing of a specially crafted input by the B.A.T.M.A.N. Advanced [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mbat.vis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m protocol dissector in Wireshark.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction at `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-bat.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m705[0m[39m`, which calls [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fprintf_chk` through the printf family of functions.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Call Stack Analysis**: The crash trace shows:[0m                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The function `QuickCheckForUnpoisonedRegion` in ASAN's memory intrinsics [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Input Characteristics**: The triggering input contains a pattern that suggests[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata in the packet being processed.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Vulnerability Type**: This appears to be a format string vulnerability where [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muser-controlled input is being used directly in a printf-family function without [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m120[0m[39m:static int hf_bat_gw_ip;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m121[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m122[0m[39m:static int hf_bat_vis_vis_orig;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m123[0m[39m:static int hf_bat_vis_version;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m124[0m[39m:static int hf_bat_vis_gwflags;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m125[0m[39m:static int hf_bat_max_tq_v22;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m126[0m[39m:static int hf_bat_max_tq_v23;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m127[0m[39m:static int hf_bat_vis_data_type;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m128[0m[39m:static int hf_bat_vis_netmask;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m129[0m[39m:static int hf_bat_vis_tq_v22;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m130[0m[39m:static int hf_bat_vis_tq_v23;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m131[0m[39m:static int hf_bat_vis_data_ip;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m132[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I have identified the root[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause and multiple security/correctness issues in the `dissect_bat_vis_v24` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Issues Identified:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Format String Vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m705[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** - The immediate crash cause:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` uses `d_output_buffer` as a format string[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `d_output_buffer` contains user-controlled packet data from [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vis_packeth_raw_data`[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Malicious format specifiers like `%x`, `%n`, `%s` in the packet are [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterpreted by fprintf[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This causes invalid memory access when fprintf tries to dereference stack [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues as pointers[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Missing Null Termination [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m668[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `vis_packeth_raw_data` buffer is filled with packet bytes but never [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull-terminated[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using it with `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m704[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `%s` format [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m687[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m causes [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mundefined behavior[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Offset Calculation Bug [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m663[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m664[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint32[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset++, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` reads [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes but post-increment only adds [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Then `offset += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` adds [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m more, resulting in [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m total instead of [0m[1;36m4[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This causes all subsequent offsets to be wrong[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Wrong Offsets in Tree Construction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m691[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m701[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses accumulated offset after raw_data reading instead of fixed packet [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstructure offsets[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Protocol fields are read from wrong packet positions[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Inappropriate Debug Code**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The entire fprintf debugging mechanism is inappropriate for production [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWireshark dissectors[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No registered header field exists for raw_data, indicating this was [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexperimental/debug code[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Comparison with v22/v23:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe v22 and v23 dissectors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m439[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m639[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m show the correct pattern:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No fprintf debugging to stderr[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Clean offset handling with fixed packet structure offsets[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Proper use of `offset = VIS_PACKET_VXX_SIZE` before processing remaining data[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No unsafe string operations on packet data[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Remove the Format String Vulnerability and Dangerous Code[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe safest and most appropriate fix is to **completely remove the dangerous fprintf[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdebugging code** and fix the offset calculation issues:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Remove lines [0m[1;36m646[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m648[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m653[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m687[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m704[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m705[0m[39m**:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the `vis_packeth_raw_data`, `d_output_buffer`, and [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vis_packeth_raw_data_size` variables[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the loop that reads raw_data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m668[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the snprintf that creates d_output_buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m687[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the fprintf call [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m704[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m705[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This eliminates the format string vulnerability entirely[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fix Offset Calculation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m663[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m664[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `vis_packeth_raw_data_size = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint32[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset++, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; offset [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+= [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - To: `offset` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjust remove this entire section since raw_data handling is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoved[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fix Tree Construction Offsets [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m680[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m702[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use a separate offset variable for tree items or reset offset to proper [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstructure positions[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Follow the v22/v23 pattern: initialize offset to [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m for tree construction[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After tree construction, set `offset = VIS_PACKET_V23_SIZE + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m + [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mraw_data_size` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbut since we're removing raw_data, just use `VIS_PACKET_V23_SIZE`[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Fix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIf raw_data must be preserved[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf there's a legitimate need to handle raw_data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough no header field is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregistered for it[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, then:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fix Offset Calculation**:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change line [0m[1;36m663[0m[39m: `vis_packeth_raw_data_size = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint32[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change line [0m[1;36m664[0m[39m: `offset += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mremove the duplicate increment[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Add Bounds Checking**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Before the loop at line [0m[1;36m668[0m[39m, add: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtvb_captured_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < vis_packeth_raw_data_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return;`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Use [0m[1;35mtvb_get_string_enc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead of manual loop**:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace lines [0m[1;36m668[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[39m with: `[0m[1;35mtvb_get_string_enc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, tvb, offset, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvis_packeth_raw_data_size, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Or use proper Wireshark API for binary data if not a string[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Add raw_data to protocol tree properly**:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use `[0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to add raw_data to the tree[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Never use fprintf for display[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Fix tree construction offsets**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use fixed offsets based on packet structure, not accumulated offset[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Detailed Implementation Steps[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove Dangerous Variables and Code**[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete declarations at lines [0m[1;36m646[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m648[0m[39m: `vis_packeth_raw_data_size`, [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vis_packeth_raw_data`, `d_output_buffer`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete initialization at line [0m[1;36m653[0m[39m: `d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete raw_data reading at lines [0m[1;36m663[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe tvb_get_uint32, size check, and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloop[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete snprintf at line [0m[1;36m687[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete the entire if block at lines [0m[1;36m704[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m705[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix Offset Handling**[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter reading the vis_packeth fields [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m660[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m662[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the offset should be at [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove the raw_data reading section entirely[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The tree construction should use fixed offsets like v23:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - offset [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: sender_ip  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - offset [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: version [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbut code uses offset [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, so there's padding[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - offset [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m: version[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - offset [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m: gw_class[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - offset [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m: tq_max[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Restructure Tree Construction**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFollowing v23 pattern, the tree items should be added at fixed offsets:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[39m* Set tree info *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    proto_item *ti;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    int tree_offset = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Use separate variable for tree construction[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ti = [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_protocol_format[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, proto_bat_vis, tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mVIS_PACKET_V23_SIZE,[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                        [0m[32m"B.A.T.M.A.N. Vis, Src: %s"[0m[39m,[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                        [0m[1;35maddress_with_resolution_to_str[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m&vis_packeth->sender_ip[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    bat_vis_tree = [0m[1;35mproto_item_add_subtree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mti, ett_bat_vis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* items *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_ipv4[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree, hf_bat_vis_vis_orig, tvb, tree_offset, [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msender_ip[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tree_offset += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree, hf_bat_vis_version, tvb, tree_offset, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tree_offset += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree, hf_bat_vis_gwflags, tvb, tree_offset, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tree_offset += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree, hf_bat_max_tq_v23, tvb, tree_offset, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[39m* Calculate offset for remaining data *[0m[35m/[0m                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Verify Remaining Data Processing**[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe remaining code at lines [0m[1;36m707[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m734[0m[39m should work correctly once offset is set [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperly.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Security**: Completely eliminates the format string vulnerability by removing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe dangerous fprintf code[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Simplicity**: Removes unnecessary experimental/debug code that has no [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorresponding header field[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Consistency**: Makes v24 dissector match the proven, safe pattern of v22 and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mv23[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Maintainability**: Reduces code complexity and removes unsafe string [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Functionality Loss**: Since there's no registered header field for raw_data[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand it's only used in a debug fprintf, removing it doesn't affect the dissector's [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactual functionality[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The core packet dissection logic remains intact[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All registered header fields are still processed correctly[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The remaining data processing loop continues to work[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The tap_queue_packet calls are preserved[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The dissect_vis_entry_v23 calls for sub-entries remain unchanged[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issues:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Crash Fix**: Eliminates the format string vulnerability that caused the SEGV[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Security**: Removes all unsafe operations on packet data[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Correctness**: Fixes offset calculation to match packet structure[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Best Practices**: Aligns with Wireshark dissector coding standards [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno stderr [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m**: Since the removed code only writes to stderr and has no registered [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol fields, removing it has no impact on Wireshark's functionality[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The v24 dissector will behave identically to v23 after this fix, which is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappropriate since they use the same vis_packet_v23 structure[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe v22 and v23 dissectors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m439[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m639[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrate the correct pattern that [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis fix implements. They cleanly process packets without any fprintf debugging or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsafe string operations.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
